#Open Military conduct window - army
custom_button = {
	name = acw_army_button_that_opens_menu 
    potential = {} 
  	trigger = { } 
  	effect = { 
		set_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
	}
}

custom_text_box = {
	name = acw_army_window_title
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
		}
		
custom_text_box = {
	name = acw_cf_perkz_avaible_cf_bg_open
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open} 
}		
		
		
custom_text_box = {
	name = acw_cf_perkz_avaible
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open} 
		}	
	}
		
custom_icon = {
	name = acw_cf_perkz_counter_icon
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open} } 
	}

		
custom_text_box = {
	name = acw_army_stratagem_text
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_stratagem_window_open_flag}} 
		}

#infantry plus button
custom_button = {
	name = acw_infantry_upgrade_plus
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
  	trigger = {	
		hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t9 }
				}
				
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t1}
					army_professionalism = 0.10 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t2}
					army_professionalism = 0.15 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t3}
					army_professionalism = 0.20 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t4}
					army_professionalism = 0.25 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t5}
					army_professionalism = 0.30 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t6}
					army_professionalism = 0.35 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t7}
					army_professionalism = 0.40 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t8}
					army_professionalism = 0.50 }
				else = {army_professionalism = 0.05}
			 }
		
  	effect = {
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t8}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.5
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t9
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
											
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t7}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.4
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
				
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t6}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.35
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
											duration = -1
											}					
					}

				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t5}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.30
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
											duration = -1
											}					
					}			
				
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t4}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.25
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
											duration = -1
											}					
					}	
				
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t3}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.20
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t2}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.15
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t2
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t1}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.10
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t2
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				if = {limit = {
								NOT = {
									OR = {	has_country_modifier	= 	acw_infantry_upgrade_t9
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t2
											has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t1
											}	
										}
								}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.05
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t1
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
	}
}

		name = acw_infantry_levels_indicator_t1
		potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already}

#downgrade button

custom_button = {
	name = acw_infantry_upgrade_minus
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
  	trigger = {	
					hidden_trigger = {
						OR = {	has_country_modifier	= 	acw_infantry_upgrade_t9
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t2
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_infantry_upgrade_t1
								}	
							}
			}
		
  	effect = {	
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t1}
						add_army_professionalism = 0.02
						hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t1	
						}	
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t2}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.07
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t2	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t1
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t3}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.1
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t3	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t2
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t4}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.125
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t4	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t5}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.15
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t5	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t6}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.175
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t7}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.2
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t7	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t8}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.22
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t8	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_infantry_upgrade_t9}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.25
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t9
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else = {}
		}
}

#cavalry plus button
custom_button = {
	name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_plus
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
  	trigger = {	
				AND = { 
					hidden_trigger = {
						NOT = {has_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t9 }
					}
					if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1}
						army_professionalism = 0.10 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2}
						army_professionalism = 0.15 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3}
						army_professionalism = 0.20 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4}
						army_professionalism = 0.25 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5}
						army_professionalism = 0.30 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6}
						army_professionalism = 0.35 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7}
						army_professionalism = 0.40 }
					else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8}
						army_professionalism = 0.50 }
					else = {army_professionalism = 0.05 }
				}
			 }
		
  	effect = {
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.5
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t9
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
											
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.4
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.35
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7
											duration = -1
											}					
					}

				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.30
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6
											duration = -1
											}					
					}			
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.25
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5
											duration = -1
											}					
					}	
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.20
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.15
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.10
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else = {
					add_army_professionalism = -0.05
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_minus
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
  	trigger = {	
					hidden_trigger = {
						OR = {	has_country_modifier	= 	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t9
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2
								has_country_modifier	=	acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1
								}	
							}
			}
		
  	effect = {	
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1}
						add_army_professionalism = 0.02
						hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1	
						}	
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.07
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t1
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.1
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t2
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.125
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t3
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.15
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t4
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.175
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t5
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.2
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t6
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.22
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t8	
						}	
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t7
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_cavalry_upgrade_t9}
					add_army_professionalism = 0.25
					hidden_effect = {
							remove_country_modifier = acw_cavalry_upgrade_t9
						}

											duration = -1
											}

#artillery plus button

custom_button = {
	name = acw_artillery_upgrade_plus
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already} 
  	trigger = {	hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {has_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t9 }
				}
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t1}
					army_professionalism = 0.10 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t2}
					army_professionalism = 0.15 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t3}
					army_professionalism = 0.20 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t4}
					army_professionalism = 0.25 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t5}
					army_professionalism = 0.30 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t6}
					army_professionalism = 0.35 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t7}
					army_professionalism = 0.40 }
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t8}
					army_professionalism = 0.50 }
				else = {army_professionalism = 0.05 }
			 }
		
  	effect = {
				if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t8}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.5
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t8
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t9
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
											
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t7}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.4
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t7
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t8
											duration = -1
											}					
					}
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t6}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.35
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t6
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t7
											duration = -1
											}					
					}

				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t5}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.30
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t5
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t6
											duration = -1
											}					
					}			
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t4}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.25
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t4
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t5
											duration = -1
											}					
					}	
				
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t3}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.20
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t3
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t4
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t2}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.15
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t2
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t3
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else_if = {limit = {has_country_modifier=acw_artillery_upgrade_t1}
					add_army_professionalism = -0.10
					hidden_effect = {
						remove_country_modifier = acw_artillery_upgrade_t1
						}
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t2
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
					
				else = {
					add_army_professionalism = -0.05
					add_country_modifier = {name = acw_artillery_upgrade_t1
											duration = -1
											}					
					}		
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = acw_infantry_levels_bar_t1a
	potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already}
	tooltip = acw_infantry_temp_skill_t1a
	trigger = {
				AND = {
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = acw_infantry_levels_bar_t1_tt
						NOT = {had_country_flag = { flag = acw_infantry_temp_skill_t1_picked
												days = 9150}}
												}
					
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = acw_infantry_levels_bar_t1_atleast3_tt
						OR = {
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t3
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t4
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t5
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t6
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t7
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t8
									has_country_modifier = acw_infantry_upgrade_t9
						}
					}
					army_professionalism = 0.2
					}
			}
	effect = { add_army_professionalism = -0.2
				add_country_modifier = { 
					name = acw_infantry_temp_skill_t1a
					duration = 5475 }
				set_country_flag = acw_infantry_temp_skill_t1_picked
			}
}

#armaments
#age of absolutism
custom_button = {
	name = acw_arm_slot_row_1_1
	tooltip = acw_arma_crouching_tiger_cannon_desc
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_1_open
						has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_2_open
						has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_3_open
						has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_4_open
							}					
					} 
  	trigger = { hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
								has_country_flag = acw_arma_s1_1
								has_country_flag = acw_arma_s2_1
								has_country_flag = acw_arma_s3_1
								has_country_flag = acw_arma_s4_1
							}	
						}
				}	
				AND = { 
						owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 674
						owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 2371
						owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 678
					}
				
				current_age = age_of_absolutism
			}
  	effect = {  	
				if = { 
					limit = {has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_1_open } 
						set_country_flag = acw_arma_s1_1
						if = {
							limit = {
								current_age = age_of_absolutism
							}
							add_country_modifier = {				
									name = acw_arma_crouching_tiger_cannon	
									duration = -1
									desc = until_end_of_age_desc
									}
							}	
						add_country_modifier = {
								name = acw_arma_slot_1_xp
								duration = -1    
								}					
						clr_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
						clr_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_1_open
					}
				else_if	= { 
					limit = {has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_2_open } 
						set_country_flag = acw_arma_s2_1
						if = {
							limit = {
								current_age = age_of_absolutism
							}
							add_country_modifier = {				
									name = acw_arma_crouching_tiger_cannon	
									duration = -1
									desc = until_end_of_age_desc
									}
							}	
						add_country_modifier = {
								name = acw_arma_slot_2_xp
								duration = -1    
								}	
						clr_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
						clr_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_2_open
					}
				else_if	= { 
					limit = {has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_3_open } 
						set_country_flag = acw_arma_s3_1
						if = {
							limit = {
								current_age = age_of_absolutism
							}
							add_country_modifier = {				
									name = acw_arma_crouching_tiger_cannon	
									duration = -1
									desc = until_end_of_age_desc
									}
							}	
						add_country_modifier = {
								name = acw_arma_slot_3_xp
								duration = -1    
								}					
						clr_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
						clr_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_3_open
					}
				else_if	= { 
					limit = {has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_4_open } 
						set_country_flag = acw_arma_s4_1
						if = {
							limit = {
								current_age = age_of_absolutism
							}
							add_country_modifier = {				
									name = acw_arma_crouching_tiger_cannon	
									duration = -1
									desc = until_end_of_age_desc
									}
							}	
						add_country_modifier = {
								name = acw_arma_slot_4_xp
								duration = -1    
								}					
						clr_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
						clr_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_4_open
					}				
			}
	frame = { number = 3
				trigger = {always = yes}
				}
}	


custom_button = {
	name = acw_arm_slot_row_1_2
	tooltip =  acw_arma_iklwa_desc
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_hd_arma_bg_open
				 OR = {
					has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_1_open
					has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_2_open
					has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_3_open
					has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_4_open
												}
					} 
  	trigger = { 
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = acw_arma_s1_2
							has_country_flag = acw_arma_s2_2

						owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 4040

						owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 1185
					}	

					current_age = age_of_absolutism
			}
  	effect = {  	
				if = { 
					limit = {has_country_flag = acw_arma_slot_1_open } 
						set_country_flag = acw_arma_s1_2
						if = {
							limit = {
								current_age = age_of_absolutism

#set the actual stratagem
custom_button = {
	name = acw_stratagem_sfp_button
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_stratagem_window_open_flag} 
  	trigger = { }
  	effect = { 
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_window_open_flag
		set_country_flag = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected
		set_country_flag = acw_stratagem_selected_already
		add_country_modifier = {
								name = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected 
								duration = -1
								    
								}
		
	}
}

#reset stratage
custom_button = {
	name = acw_stratagem_discontinue_button
    potential = {	AND = {
						acw_has_stratagem = yes
						has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
						}		
				} 
  	trigger = { }
  	effect = { 
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_selected_already
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_dod_selected
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_trc_selected
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_rom_selected
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_has_selected
		clr_country_flag = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected	
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_selected 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t1 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t2 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t3 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t4 

		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_selected 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t1 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t2 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t3 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t4 

		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_selected 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t1 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t2 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t3 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t4 

		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t1 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t2 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t3 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t4 

		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_selected 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t1 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t2 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t3 
		remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t4 
	}
}

#level up
custom_button = {
	name = acw_stratagem_level_up_button
    potential = {
					AND = {
						acw_has_stratagem = yes
						has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
						}
				}
				
  	trigger = { AND = {
					#	army_professionalism = 0.75
						hidden_trigger ={ 
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t4
									has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t4
									has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t4
									has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t4
									has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t4
								}
							}
						}
				}
			}
  	effect = { 
	#remove previous tier modifier, add next tier
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t3 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t3
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_sfp_t4
									duration = -1
									    
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t2 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t2
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_sfp_t3
									duration = -1
									    
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t1 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_t1
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_sfp_t2
									duration = -1
									    
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_sfp_selected
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_sfp_t1
									duration = -1
									  
								}
							}
								
		#remove previous tier modifier, add next tier
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t3 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t3
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_dod_t4
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t2 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t2
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_dod_t3
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = {  has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t1 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_t1
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_dod_t2
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_selected }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_dod_selected
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_dod_t1
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
								
		#remove previous tier modifier, add next tier
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t3 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t3
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_trc_t4
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t2 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t2
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_trc_t3
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t1 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_t1
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_trc_t2
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_selected }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_trc_selected
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_trc_t1
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}

		#remove previous tier modifier, add next tier
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t3 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t3
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_has_t4
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t2 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t2
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_has_t3
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t1 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_t1
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_has_t2
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_selected }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_has_selected
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_has_t1
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
								
		#remove previous tier modifier, add next tier
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t3 }
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t3
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_rom_t4
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t2 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t2
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_rom_t3
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t1 }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_t1
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_rom_t2
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
		IF = { limit = { has_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_selected }
							add_army_professionalism = -0.5
							remove_country_modifier = acw_stratagem_rom_selected
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_stratagem_rom_t1
									duration = -1
									
								}
							}
	
		}
	
	}

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_up_one_page
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open}
	trigger = { 
						hidden_trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_3}}
				}
	effect = {		IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2}
							clr_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2
							set_country_flag = acw_cf_page_3
							}
				
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1}
							clr_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1
							set_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2
							}
	}
}	


custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_down_one_page
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open}
	trigger = { 
						hidden_trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1}}
				}
	effect = {		IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_3}
							clr_country_flag = acw_cf_page_3
							set_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2
							}
				
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2}
							clr_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2
							set_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1
							}
		}
}

#company 1 - suttlers (of catan) / french suttlers (dont ask)

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_company_1
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1
				 }
	tooltip = acw_cf_company_1_tt
					
	trigger = { hidden_trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_picked}}
				acw_cf_perkz_avaible_is = yes}		
				
	effect = {		
					
					acw_cf_decrease_perkz = yes
					
					IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_1_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot1 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s1_1 }
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_2_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot2 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s2_1 }	
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_3_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot3 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s3_1 }	
					ELSE = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_4_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot4 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s4_1 }		

					set_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_picked
					
					IF = {limit = {primary_culture = francien} 
							add_country_modifier = {
									name = acw_cf_company_1_mod_1
									duration = -1
												}
							}					
					ELSE = 	 {
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_1_mod
										duration = -1
													}	
												
											
													
					}		
							
				}
	
	frame = { number = 8
				trigger = {primary_culture = francien}
				}
	
	frame = { number = 1
				trigger = {always = yes}
				}
}	

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_company_1_s_a
	tooltip = acw_cf_company_1_s_a_tt
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_1
				} 
	trigger = { 
		hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_s_a_picked
						has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_s_b_picked
						}
					}
				}	
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = acw_cf_company_must_be_unlocked
					has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_picked
					}
					acw_cf_perkz_avaible_is = yes
				}	
				
	effect = {		
					set_country_flag = acw_cf_company_1_s_a_picked
					add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_1_a_mod
										duration = -1
													}	
					acw_cf_decrease_perkz = yes
				}
				
	frame = { number = 2
				trigger = {always = yes}
				}
}

							}					
												
												
					}

				trigger = {always = yes}

#scouts

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_company_6
	tooltip = acw_cf_company_6_tt
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open 
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_2
				} 
	trigger = { hidden_trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_6_picked}}
				acw_cf_perkz_avaible_is = yes}		
				
	effect = {		acw_cf_decrease_perkz = yes
					
					IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_1_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot1 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s1_6}
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_2_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot2 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s2_6 }	
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_3_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot3 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s3_6 }	
					ELSE = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_4_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot4 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s4_6 }		

					set_country_flag = acw_cf_company_6_picked
					
						IF = {limit = {has_estate = estate_cossacks} 
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod
										duration = -1
													}
								}
						ELSE_IF = {limit = {culture_group = east_slavic} 
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod_1
										duration = -1
													}
								}		
						ELSE_IF = {limit = {primary_culture = mexican} 
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod_2
										duration = -1
													}
								}		
								
						ELSE_IF = {limit = {culture_group = carpathian}
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod_3
										duration = -1
													}
								}		
						
						ELSE_IF = {limit = {primary_culture = maori}
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod_4
										duration = -1
													}
								}
						
						ELSE = 	 {
								add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_6_mod_5
										duration = -1
													}	
							}				
				}
	
	frame = { number = 8
				trigger = {
								has_estate = estate_cossacks
				}
			}
	frame = { number = 9
				trigger = {
								culture_group = east_slavic
				}
			}
	frame = { number = 10
				trigger = {
								primary_culture = mexican
				}
			}
	frame = { number = 11
				trigger = {
								culture_group = carpathian
				}
			}
	frame = { number = 12
				trigger = {
								primary_culture = maori
				}
			}
	
	frame = { number = 1
				trigger = {always = yes}
				}
			
}

				trigger = {primary_culture = japanese}
				}

				trigger = {always = yes}
				}

						has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_10_s_ab_picked

					}

			}
				
	effect = {	set_country_flag = acw_cf_company_10_s_aa_picked
				add_country_modifier = {
										name = acw_cf_company_10_aa_mod
										duration = -1

				acw_cf_decrease_perkz = yes
				}

custom_button = {
	name = acw_cf_company_11
	tooltip = acw_cf_company_11_tt
    potential = {has_country_flag = acw_background_open_already
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_bg_open 
				 has_country_flag = acw_cf_page_3
				} 
	trigger = { hidden_trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_company_11_picked}}
				any_owned_province = { trade_goods = slaves }
				acw_cf_perkz_avaible_is = yes
				}		
				
	effect = {	acw_cf_decrease_perkz = yes
					
					IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_1_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot1 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s1_11}
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_2_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot2 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s2_11 }	
					ELSE_IF = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_3_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot3 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s3_11 }	
					ELSE = {limit = {has_country_flag = acw_cf_slot_4_open}
										acw_remove_all_from_slot4 = yes
										set_country_flag = acw_cf_s4_11 }		

					set_country_flag = acw_cf_company_11_picked
	
	
	
					IF = {limit = {culture_group = persian}
										add_country_modifier = {
											name = acw_cf_company_11_mod
											duration = -1
													}
										}
					ELSE= {					
										add_country_modifier = {
											name = acw_cf_company_11_mod_1
											duration = -1
													}
									}
		
					}
	
	frame = { number = 8
				trigger = {culture_group = persian}
				}
	
	frame = { number = 1
				trigger = {always = yes}
				}
}
